NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

of V SAHUL HAMITHU on 5th March 2010.
V. VINITH KUMAR.
Tiruchirappalli, 29th May 2015.

PUBLIC NOTICE
R. Karthikeyan, a male child born to Ramasamy, C., born on 13th February 1991 residing at 111, Main Road,
Kavulpalayam, Perambalur District, has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery on
13th December 2013 at Shivam Vishva Multispeciality Hospital, Bengaluru Surgery by Dr. V. Jayaraman
(Reg. No. 32070), former Professor and Head Department of Burns Plastic and Reconstructive Surgery, Kilpauk Medical
Hospital, Chennai-600 010. By this I may be treated as a female and shall henceforth be known as NAYANTHARA, R.

Perambalur,

KARTHIKEYAN, R.

26th May 2015.

P. Sathish Kumar alias P. Satish Kumar was born as a male child of V. PALANI on 27th December 1995 residing
at No. 33, 15, Gugan Street, Kodambakkam, Chennai-600 024. After an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery she has
been living as a female (reference Dr. V. JAYARAMAN, MS. MCH, MNAMS, Dip, N.B., Phd., FICS. Former Professor and
Head, Department of Burns, Plastic and Reconstructive Surgery, Kilpauk Medical College Hospital, Chennai-600 010. The
thorough clinical examination under Dr. V. JAYARAMAN, MS. MCH, MNAMS, Dip, N.B., Phd., FICS. shows that I could
be treated as a female P. SATHISH KUMAR alias P. SATISH KUMAR shall henceforth be known as P. SANJANA.

Chennai,

P. SATHISH KUMAR alias P. SATISH KUMAR.

29th May 2015.
